On New Years Eve at about 1:30 PM I managed to lock the keys in a friend's borrow BMW X5 in a very remote location. I tossed my backpack onto the passenger seat (with the key zipped into an outside pocket) and closed the door.  The pack fell onto it's face and managed to lock the vehicle just as the door closed. Tuesdays in the 1st and 3rd if the month is government day, which can be visited in once per month, you'll receive your essentials like meats, cheeses, etc. Wednesday, Fridays, and Saturdays are panty days and you can visit multiple times per month and when available can receive dog food and tolietrees. < review>
Take my advice and go to a BOARD CERTIFIED plastic surgeon, and here's why.  I had lipo many years ago and was quite happy with the results.  Earlier this year, I decided to have it done again; in the same area (tummy) as well as additional areas (love handles, flanks and hips).  I initially was interested in their "special" pricing but was told that it didn't apply to me since I had had lipo previously and there were some corrective measures that had to be done which would cost more.  Ok, fair enough.  So instead of paying the special price, I paid almost double that amount.  Like you, I was very encouraged by the reviews that I read about Pacific Lipo and was very excited about the results, particularly since I was their definition of an ideal candidate (not overweight, just isolated stubborn areas).  My sensible side was telling me not to proceed with any of the "lipo only" practices cropping up all over the place, but rather go to a board certified plastic surgeon who, believe it or not, would have charged the same amount of money.  But....those Pacific Lipo reviews!  They were very encouraging so I decided to go with Pacific Lipo and in doing so, lost $7,000.00 and look almost EXACTLY the same as I did before I walked in the door.  And that's not the worst of it.  The worst of it is this.....as I went for my 1 month, 2 month, 3 month, 4 month and 5 month follow up visits and voiced my concerns about the lack of results I was seeing, I was told either I still had swelling (and to be patient) or what I was referring to was skin (which I confirmed with three other doctors that it was, in fact, fat and not skin) or that if changes weren't visible by the next follow up, we could explore some laser techniques.  At the 6 month follow up, I put my foot down and expressed my unhappiness with the results.  Did the Doc respond by saying "I'm sorry you are unhappy, let's review some options to see how we can make this right"?  Nope.  Did he say "ok, there are other techniques we can try to achieve reasonable results, including the laser techniques we discussed previously"?  Nope.  He promptly directed me to refer to the agreement that I signed where it stated that results are measured by a "50 % measure" meaning if your results are 50% better than when you walked through the door, he'd done his job and basically you're out of luck.  He also used the fact that I had previously had lipo as an excuse (ummm...yeah.  isn't that why you told me I had to pay more to correct it?) as he slinked into another patient's room to avoid having to continue the conversation with me.  I can tell you in NO UNCERTAIN terms that my improvement is FAR BELOW 50%.  When no one (and I mean no one including my best friend who did not see me until 4 moths after the surgery) notices that your body shape is even remotely improved, I would call that closer to ZERO percent.  I can tell you from experience that a board certifed surgeon would have never let me walk out of that door without making sure that I was happy, or at the very least exploring additional measures to achieve reasonable results.  Nope.  This guy basically told me not to let the door hit me on the way out.  As a final note, I'd like to point out that I have no doubt that the positive reviews on this site are true and many people achieved the results they expected, but I would just recommend you consider the fact that if you are going to spend that kind of money, go with a doctor who is a BOARD CERTIFIED plastic surgeon.  In many ways, it is a form of insurance for your investment because they will ALWAYS stand behind their work in my experience.</review>

< text>
I was seen at Lodi Western Dental on Tuesday and Wednesday this week.  Having a phobia about going to the dentist, I put off making an appointment for several years.
Vanessa, the finance coordinator, was very nice, explained my options and answered all of my questions with a smile.  The oral surgeons and dental assistants were also very nice and gentle, which convinced me that my phobia & fears were unnecessary.
But the person that stands out most as making this an excellent experience for me two days in a row was the dental hygienist.  He was very professional, yet friendly and compassionate.  I needed an extensive deep cleaning & he did an excellent job.  First, he made sure I was relaxed and put my mind at ease by explaining everything ahead of time.  He adequately numbed my mouth so I didn't feel any discomfort, and he explained everything step by step so there were no surprises.  He reviewed the home care instructions with me several times both days, making sure I fully understood his instructions.  It is obvious that Hassan loves his chosen field of expertise.
I will not postpone having cleanings done in the future, as long as he is the hygienist!
Overall, from start to finish this was an excellent experience.  I will no longer postpone dental appointments based on my phobias.<//text>
